  ---
  RasoSpeak: Complete Architectural Redesign Blueprint

  From Hackathon Prototype to Production-Grade Autonomous AI Operating System

  ---
  1. BRUTALLY HONEST ARCHITECTURAL ASSESSMENT

  Why the Current System is NOT Truly Agentic

  The current RasoSpeak is a FastAPI monolith with prompt wrappers masquerading 
  as agents. Here's the surgical breakdown:

  Critical Failures

  1. "Agents" Are Just Prompt Wrappers
  - BaseAgent defines initialize() with zero abstract methods beyond that
  - Every "agent" is literally just an LLM API wrapper with a __init__ and one
  method
  - CoachingAgent.ask() вҶ’ calls LLM вҶ’ returns response. That's not an agent,
  that's a function.
  - No planning, no memory of prior actions within the agent, no
  self-reflection, no tool use beyond calling one LLM

  2. No Real Orchestration
  - main.py initializes agents sequentially in lifespan()
  - All agents share one global agents dict in api/state.py
  - Communication is implicit: agents call each other via set_second_brain() /
  set_shared_memory() вҖ” direct coupling
  - No event bus, no message queues, no pub/sub

  3. Shared Mutable Globals Are a Time Bomb
  # api/state.py
  agents: dict[str, Any] = {}  # Global mutable state
  _ws_session_tokens: dict[str, str] = {}  # In-memory tokens
  - This crashes under concurrent requests
  - No thread safety, no isolation
  - Memory grows unbounded

  4. JSON Persistence is Unacceptable for Production
  - memory/conversations.json, memory/facts.json, memory/profile.json
  - No transactions, no schema, no versioning
  - Concurrent writes corrupt data
  - No backup strategy, no encryption at rest

  5. No User Isolation
  - All users share the same agents dict
  - No tenant context propagation
  - Session tokens stored in-memory with no Redis backing

  6. No Fault Tolerance
  - No retries, no circuit breakers
  - If LLM API fails, the request fails completely
  - No fallback providers configured

  7. No Observability
  - Basic logging.info() statements
  - No distributed tracing
  - No token usage tracking per user
  - No cost analytics

  8. No Durable Execution
  - If the server crashes mid-session, all state is lost
  - No workflow state persistence
  - No checkpoint/resume capability

  What Should Be DELETED Entirely

  Component: api/state.py global agents dict
  Why Delete: Source of all race conditions
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Component: JSON files in memory/
  Why Delete: No transactional integrity
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Component: session_memory_agent.py
  Why Delete: In-memory session state without persistence
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Component: shared_memory_agent.py
  Why Delete: Mutable global state sharing
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Component: All .json persistence
  Why Delete: Replace with PostgreSQL
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Component: The current "agent" pattern entirely
  Why Delete: Agents are just LLM wrappers

  What is Worth PRESERVING

  Component: agents/llm_client.py
  Why Keep: Solid multi-provider abstraction
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  ---
  2. WHAT A REAL AGENT ACTUALLY IS

  Formal Definition: Production-Grade Autonomous AI Agent

  A real autonomous agent is a system that:

  AGENT = (GOAL, PERCEPT, ACTION, MODEL, MEMORY, TOOLS, PLANNER, REFLECTOR)

  Where:
  - GOAL: Desired end state (explicit or implicit)
  - PERCEPT: Observes environment state
  - ACTION: Executes tools/functions that change environment
  - MODEL: Internal world model updated by observations
  - MEMORY: Stores experiences, facts, procedures across time
  - TOOLS: External capabilities (search, compute, APIs, code)
  - PLANNER: Decomposes goals into subgoals
  - REFLECTOR: Evaluates actions, updates strategy

  Real Agent vs Fake Agent Comparison

  Property: Goals
  Fake Agent (Current): None
  Real Agent: Explicit goal state with success criteria
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Property: Planning
  Fake Agent (Current): None
  Real Agent: Replans when environment changes
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Property: Memory
  Fake Agent (Current): Static context injection
  Real Agent: Episodic + semantic + procedural memory
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  Workflows vs Agents vs Cognition Loops

  WORKFLOW: f(x) вҶ’ y (deterministic pipeline)
  AGENT: Perceive вҶ’ Plan вҶ’ Act вҶ’ Perceive (with loops)

  The current system is a workflow (linear pipeline). It needs to become a
  multi-agent cognition platform.

  3. NEW TARGET ARCHITECTURE

  3.1 Architecture Overview

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”җ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Kubernetes   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  GPU Nodes   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Ingress     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   Service      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (EKS/GKE)   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  (vLLM)      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Controller  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   Mesh         в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”ҳ

  3.2 Core Services Specification

  A. API Gateway Service

  Responsibility: Entry point for all client requests, authentication, rate
  limiting, routing

  Technology: Kong Gateway or Traefik

  APIs:
  - REST endpoints for CRUD operations
  - WebSocket endpoint for real-time agent streaming
  - gRPC for internal service-to-service communication

  Communication Pattern: Stateless, horizontal scaling behind load balancer

  Scaling Strategy: Horizontal pod autoscaling based on CPU/connection count

  Storage Strategy: No local storage; all state in Redis/PostgreSQL

  Failure Handling: Circuit breaker to backend services, graceful degradation

  B. Agent Runtime Service

  Responsibility: Manages agent lifecycle, scheduling, communication, and state

  Technology: Custom service built on Temporal SDK + custom agent framework

  APIs:
  service AgentRuntime {
    rpc CreateAgent(CreateAgentRequest) returns (Agent);
    rpc SendMessage(AgentMessage) returns (stream AgentResponse);
    rpc GetAgentState(AgentId) returns (AgentState);
    rpc TerminateAgent(AgentId) returns (google.protobuf.Empty);
    rpc SubscribeToAgent(AgentId) returns (stream AgentEvent);
  }

  Communication Pattern: gRPC for internal, WebSocket for clients

  Scaling Strategy: Agent pools per tenant, Kubernetes HPA on active agent count

  Storage Strategy: Agent state persisted to PostgreSQL via Temporal workflows

  Failure Handling: Temporal handles workflow completion/retry; dead-letter
  queue for failed messages

  C. Planner Service

  Responsibility: Decomposes user goals into executable task graphs

  Technology: Dedicated service with LangGraph for graph-based planning

  APIs:
  # Input: "Help me prepare for my ML interview next month"
  # Output: Task dependency graph

  class TaskGraph:
      root_goal: Goal
      tasks: List[TaskNode]  # id, description, dependencies, tools_needed, 
  agent_type
      estimated_duration: timedelta
      priority: int

  Communication Pattern: Async messaging via NATS, REST for synchronous queries

  Scaling Strategy: Stateless, horizontal scaling

  Storage Strategy: Task graphs stored in PostgreSQL with versioning

  Failure Handling: If subtask fails, replan around it (reflexive replanning)

  D. Memory Service (Critical вҖ” Full Redesign)

  Responsibility: Hierarchical memory storage and retrieval across all time
  scales

  Technology: PostgreSQL + pgvector + Redis + Qdrant (tiered)

  APIs:
  service MemoryService {
    rpc StoreEpisodic(EpisodicMemory) returns (MemoryId);
    rpc StoreSemantic(SemanticMemory) returns (MemoryId);
    rpc StoreWorking(WorkingMemory) returns (MemoryId);
    rpc Retrieve(RetrieveRequest) returns (RetrieveResponse);
    rpc Consolidate(ConsolidateRequest) returns (ConsolidateResponse);
    rpc Summarize(SummarizeRequest) returns (Summary);
    rpc Evict(EvictRequest) returns (EvictionResult);
  }

  Memory Hierarchy:
  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ WORKING MEMORY (Redis)                                  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Current conversation context                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Active task state                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Token budget management                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - TTL: Session duration (5-60 min)                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Capacity: ~128K tokens per session                    в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ EPISODIC MEMORY (PostgreSQL)                           в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Complete conversation transcripts                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Action-outcome sequences                              в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Emotional tone markers                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Temporal context                                     в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - TTL: 90 days, then archive or summarize              в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ SEMANTIC MEMORY (PostgreSQL + pgvector)                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Extracted facts and beliefs                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - User preferences and patterns                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Knowledge graph (Neo4j or PostgreSQL recursive)      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Embedded for semantic search                         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - TTL: Long-term, with decay scoring                  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ PROCEDURAL MEMORY (PostgreSQL)                         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Learned agent behaviors                              в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Tool use patterns                                    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Strategy effectiveness scores                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Compiled into agent capabilities                     в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ ARCHIVAL MEMORY (Qdrant + S3)                         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Compressed/summarized old episodes                   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Vector embeddings for retrieval                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - Documents and media                                  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ - TTL: Indefinite (user-controlled deletion)          в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Communication Pattern: gRPC for high-frequency operations, event-driven for
  background tasks

  Scaling Strategy: Redis Cluster for working memory, PostgreSQL read replicas,
  Qdrant for vectors

  Failure Handling: Redis persistence (AOF + RDB), PostgreSQL replication,
  Qdrant snapshotting

  E. Tool Execution Service

  Responsibility: Sandboxed execution of agent tools (code, search, APIs)

  Technology: Isolated microservices with Docker containers or WebAssembly
  sandbox

  APIs:
  service ToolExecution {
    rpc ExecuteTool(ToolRequest) returns (ToolResponse);
    rpc ExecuteStreaming(stream ToolChunk) returns (stream ToolChunk);
    rpc ListTools(TenantId) returns (ToolList);
    rpc RegisterTool(ToolDefinition) returns (ToolId);
  }

  Communication Pattern: gRPC with 30s timeout per tool call

  Scaling Strategy: Kubernetes HPA based on pending tool executions

  Storage Strategy: Tool execution logs to PostgreSQL, artifacts to S3

  Failure Handling: Timeout enforcement, resource limits (CPU/memory), circuit
  breaker per tool type

  F. Workflow Engine

  Responsibility: Durable execution of complex multi-step workflows

  Technology: Temporal (non-negotiable вҖ” this is the backbone)

  Why Temporal over alternatives:

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ        Feature         в”Ӯ Temporal в”Ӯ LangGraph в”Ӯ Prefect в”Ӯ Airflow в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө

  Temporal Architecture:
  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ TEMPORAL CLUSTER                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Frontend     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ History      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Matching     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (gRPC API)   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Service      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Service      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ              Persistence Layer (Cassandra)        в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ

  APIs: Use Temporal Go/Python SDK directly, expose workflow triggers via REST

  G. Event Bus

  Responsibility: Asynchronous communication between all services

  Technology: NATS JetStream (not Kafka вҖ” see comparison)

  Feature: Latency
  NATS JetStream: <1ms
  Kafka: 5-20ms
  RabbitMQ: 1-5ms
  Redis Streams: <1ms
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Feature: Ordering
  NATS JetStream: Per-subject
  Kafka: Per-partition
  RabbitMQ: Per-queue
  Redis Streams: Per-stream
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Feature: At-least-once
  NATS JetStream: вң“
  Kafka: вң“

  Redis Streams: вң“
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Feature: Exactly-once

  Subject Hierarchy:

  APIs:
  service RAGService {
    rpc IndexDocument(IndexRequest) returns (IndexResponse);
    rpc Search(SearchRequest) returns (SearchResponse);
    rpc HybridSearch(HybridRequest) returns (HybridResponse);
    rpc UpdateCollection(CollectionConfig) returns (Empty);
    rpc DeleteCollection(CollectionName) returns (Empty);
  }

  I. Session Service

  Responsibility: User session management, authentication, context

  Technology: Redis for active sessions, PostgreSQL for session history

  APIs:
  service SessionService {
    rpc CreateSession(CreateSessionRequest) returns (Session);
    rpc GetSession(SessionId) returns (Session);
    rpc UpdateSession(Session) returns (Session);
    rpc ListUserSessions(UserId) returns (SessionList);
    rpc TerminateSession(SessionId) returns (Empty);
    rpc RefreshToken(RefreshRequest) returns (TokenPair);
  }

  J. Identity Service

  Responsibility: Authentication, authorization, RBAC, tenant management

  Technology: Custom JWT-based auth with PostgreSQL for identity storage, Vault
  for secrets

  APIs:
  service IdentityService {
    rpc Authenticate(AuthRequest) returns (TokenPair);
    rpc Authorize(AuthzRequest) returns (AuthzDecision);
    rpc CreateUser(CreateUserRequest) returns (User);
    rpc AssignRole(AssignRoleRequest) returns (Empty);
    rpc CreateTenant(CreateTenantRequest) returns (Tenant);
    rpc ListTenantUsers(TenantId) returns (UserList);
  }

  K. Speech Service

  Responsibility: Speech-to-text and text-to-speech

  Technology:
  - STT: Whisper (self-hosted via vLLM) OR Deepgram/NVIDIA NeMo
  - TTS: Cartesia, ElevenLabs, or self-hosted via Coqui

  APIs:
  service SpeechService {
    rpc Transcribe(AudioChunk) returns (Transcription);
    rpc TranscribeStream(stream AudioChunk) returns (stream Transcription);
    rpc Synthesize(SynthesizeRequest) returns (AudioResponse);
    rpc SynthesizeStream(SynthesizeRequest) returns (stream AudioChunk);
  }

  L. Analytics Service

  Responsibility: Observability, AI telemetry, cost tracking

  Technology: OpenTelemetry + Prometheus + Grafana + Langfuse

  ---
  4. TRUE MULTI-AGENT ARCHITECTURE

  4.1 Agent Types and Hierarchy

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ                    AGENT HIERARCHY                              в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ  LEVEL 0: SUPERVISOR (Meta-Agent)                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ - Interprets user intent                                 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ - Selects active agent team                             в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ - Monitors overall goal progress                        в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ - Handles cross-agent conflicts                          в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ - Triggers reflection cycles                            в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ  LEVEL 1: PLANNING AGENTS                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   Planner   в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Researcher в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ    Coordinator          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   Agent     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   Agent     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ    Agent                в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (Goal       в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (Gather     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ (Orchestrates          в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Decompos.) в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Info)      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Sub-agents)           в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ  LEVEL 2: EXECUTION AGENTS                                       в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ Coaching  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   QA      в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ   RAG     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Search   в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Agent    в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Agent    в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Agent    в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Agent    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ(Speech    в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ(Question  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ(Document  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ(Web       в”Ӯ в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ  LEVEL 3: UTILITY AGENTS                                         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ в”Ӯ

  4.2 Agent Communication Protocol

  Agent Message Format

  message AgentMessage {
    string message_id = 1;
    string sender_id = 2;
    string sender_type = 3;  // agent, service, user, system
    string receiver_id = 4;  // specific agent or "broadcast"
    MessageType type = 5;
    bytes payload = 6;  // Any structured message
    map<string, string> metadata = 7;
    uint64 timestamp_ns = 8;
    string trace_id = 9;
    string span_id = 10;
  }

  enum MessageType {
    REQUEST = 0;
    RESPONSE = 1;
    EVENT = 2;
    BROADCAST = 3;
    DELEGATION = 4;
    RESULT = 5;
    ERROR = 6;
    HEARTBEAT = 7;
  }

  Agent Lifecycle State Machine

                      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
                      в”Ӯ  CREATED    в”Ӯ
                      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

                      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

             в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ                   в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ receive_goal()           в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ              в–ј                          в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ       в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                   в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ PLANNING    в”Ӯв—„в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ӯ

             в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ subtask_complete         в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ              в–ј                          в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ       в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ                   в”Ӯ
             в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ VERIFYING    в”Ӯв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
             в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

             в”Ӯ              в–ј

             в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–әв”Ӯ  TERMINATED в”Ӯ

  4.3 Agent Runtime Implementation

  # services/agent-runtime/src/agent_runtime/core/agent.py
  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  from typing import Any, Optional
  from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  from enum import Enum
  import asyncio
  import uuid
  from datetime import datetime

  class AgentState(Enum):
      CREATED = "created"
      IDLE = "idle"
      PLANNING = "planning"
      EXECUTING = "executing"
      VERIFYING = "verifying"
      REFLECTING = "reflecting"
      COMPLETED = "completed"
      SUSPENDED = "suspended"
      TERMINATED = "terminated"
      FAILED = "failed"

  @dataclass
  class AgentConfig:
      agent_id: str
      agent_type: str
      tenant_id: str
      user_id: str
      capabilities: list[str]
      tools: list[str]
      max_retries: int = 3
      timeout_seconds: int = 300
      memory_budget_tokens: int = 128_000

  @dataclass
  class Goal:
      goal_id: str
      description: str
      success_criteria: list[str]
      priority: int = 0
      deadline: Optional[datetime] = None
      metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

  @dataclass
  class ExecutionContext:
      """Complete execution context passed to agent on each cycle"""
      goal: Goal
      working_memory: dict[str, Any]
      episodic_memory: list[dict]
      semantic_memory: dict[str, Any]
      available_tools: list[str]
      token_budget: int
      trace_id: str
      cycle_number: int = 0
      confidence: float = 1.0

  @dataclass
  class AgentResponse:
      message_id: str
      agent_id: str
      state: AgentState
      reasoning: str  # Chain of thought
      actions_taken: list[dict]  # Tools used
      output: Any
      confidence: float
      needs_handoff: bool = False
      handoff_target: Optional[str] = None

  class BaseAgent(ABC):
      """Abstract base for all production agents"""

      def __init__(self, config: AgentConfig):
          self.config = config
          self.state = AgentState.CREATED
          self.execution_history: list[AgentResponse] = []
          self.beliefs: dict[str, Any] = {}

      @abstractmethod
      async def plan(self, context: ExecutionContext) -> list["TaskNode"]:
          """Decompose goal into task graph"""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      async def execute(self, task: "TaskNode", context: ExecutionContext) ->
  dict:
          """Execute a single task node"""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      async def verify(self, output: Any, goal: Goal) -> tuple[bool, str]:
          """Verify output meets success criteria"""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      async def reflect(self, context: ExecutionContext, output: Any) -> dict:
          """Self-evaluate and update beliefs"""
          pass

      async def run_cognition_loop(self, goal: Goal) -> AgentResponse:
          """Main cognition loop: Plan вҶ’ Execute вҶ’ Verify вҶ’ Reflect"""
          context = await self._build_context(goal)

          for cycle in range(self.config.max_retries):
              context.cycle_number = cycle

              # PLAN
              self.state = AgentState.PLANNING
              tasks = await self.plan(context)

              # EXECUTE
              self.state = AgentState.EXECUTING
              outputs = []
              for task in tasks:
                  if task.depends_on and not all(d.completed for d in
  task.depends_on):
                      continue  # Wait for dependencies
                  output = await self.execute(task, context)
                  task.completed = True
                  task.output = output
                  outputs.append(output)

              # VERIFY
              self.state = AgentState.VERIFYING
              verified, verification_msg = await self.verify(outputs, goal)

              if verified:
                  self.state = AgentState.COMPLETED
                  break

              # REFLECT & REPLAN
              self.state = AgentState.REFLECTING
              reflection = await self.reflect(context, outputs)
              context.confidence *= reflection.get("confidence_multiplier", 0.9)

              if cycle < self.config.max_retries - 1:
                  context = await self._rebuild_context(context, reflection)

          return AgentResponse(
              message_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
              agent_id=self.config.agent_id,
              state=self.state,
              reasoning=self._build_chain_of_thought(),
              actions_taken=[t.__dict__ for t in tasks],
              output=outputs[-1] if outputs else None,
              confidence=context.confidence
          )

  ---
  5. COGNITIVE ARCHITECTURE

  5.1 Memory Architecture

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  prepare    в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ вҶ’ Subgoal 2 в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ вҶ’ Action: RAG      в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Token Budget: 128K tokens (sliding window)                    в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  TTL: Session duration (5-60 min inactivity timeout)          в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  Persistence: Redis AOF + PostgreSQL checkpoint every 30s      в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ   в”Ӯ

  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  5.2 Memory Consolidation Pipeline

  # services/memory/src/consolidation/pipeline.py
  class MemoryConsolidationPipeline:
      """
      Automatic memory consolidation that runs periodically.
      Implements memory pyramid: working вҶ’ episodic вҶ’ semantic вҶ’ procedural
      """

      async def run_consolidation(self, user_id: str):
          # 1. WORKING вҶ’ EPISODIC: Checkpoint working memory to episodic
          await self.checkpoint_working_memory(user_id)

          # 2. EPISODIC вҶ’ SEMANTIC: Extract facts from recent episodes
          await self.extract_facts(user_id)

          # 3. SEMANTIC CLEANUP: Merge duplicates, update confidence
          await self.consolidate_semantic(user_id)

          # 4. PROCEDURAL EXTRACTION: Identify new patterns/behaviors
          await self.extract_procedures(user_id)

          # 5. SUMMARIZATION: Compress old episodes
          await self.summarize_old_episodes(user_id)

          # 6. EVICTION: Remove low-value, old memories
          await self.evict_low_value(user_id)

      async def checkpoint_working_memory(self, user_id: str):
          """Move working memory to episodic storage"""
          working = await self.redis.get(f"working:{user_id}")
          if not working:
              return

          episode = EpisodicMemory(
              user_id=user_id,
              content=working,
              importance=self._calculate_importance(working),
              emotional_tone=self._detect_emotional_tone(working),
              topics=self._extract_topics(working),
              created_at=datetime.utcnow(),
              episode_type="conversation"
          )

          await self.db.insert(episode)
          # Don't delete working memory yet - it may still be needed

      async def extract_facts(self, user_id: str):
          """Extract factual knowledge from recent episodes"""
          recent = await self.db.query(
              EpisodicMemory,
              user_id=user_id,
              since=datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=7),
              order_by=desc(EpisodicMemory.created_at)
          )

          # Use LLM to extract facts
          extraction_prompt = f"""
          Extract factual statements from this conversation.
          Return JSON array of facts with confidence scores.
          
          Conversation:
          {self._serialize_episodes(recent)}
          """

          facts = await self.llm.extract_json(extraction_prompt)

          for fact in facts:
              semantic = SemanticMemory(
                  user_id=user_id,
                  content=fact["statement"],
                  embedding=self.embed(fact["statement"]),
                  confidence=fact["confidence"],
                  source_episodes=[e.id for e in recent],
                  fact_type=self._classify_fact(fact),
                  importance=fact.get("importance", 0.5),
                  last_accessed=datetime.utcnow(),
                  access_count=0
              )
              await self.db.upsert(semantic)

  5.3 Memory Retrieval Pipeline

  # services/memory/src/retrieval/engine.py
  class MemoryRetrievalEngine:
      """
      Multi-stage memory retrieval with hybrid search.
      """

      async def retrieve(
          self,
          user_id: str,
          query: str,
          context_window: int = 10,
          max_tokens: int = 8000
      ) -> RetrievalResult:

          # 1. PARSE QUERY INTENT
          intent = await self._parse_intent(query)

          # 2. MULTI-STAGE RETRIEVAL
          results = {}

          # Working memory (immediate context)
          if intent.needs_working:
              results["working"] = await self._retrieve_working(
                  user_id, query, context_window
              )

          # Episodic memory (recent events)
          if intent.needs_episodic:
              results["episodic"] = await self._retrieve_episodic(
                  user_id, query,
                  days_back=intent.days_back or 90
              )

          # Semantic memory (facts/knowledge)
          if intent.needs_semantic:
              results["semantic"] = await self._retrieve_semantic(
                  user_id, query
              )

          # Procedural memory (how to act)
          if intent.needs_procedural:
              results["procedural"] = await self._retrieve_procedural(
                  user_id, intent.task_type
              )

          # 3. RERANK BY RELEVANCE + RECENCY + IMPORTANCE
          reranked = self._rerank(results, query)

          # 4. CONSTRUCT CONTEXT WITHIN TOKEN BUDGET
          context = self._construct_context(
              reranked,
              max_tokens=max_tokens
          )

          # 5. ADD MEMORY METADATA
          return RetrievalResult(
              context=context,
              sources=reranked,
              retrieval_method="hybrid",
              token_count=self.tokenizer.count(context),
              memory_coverage=self._calculate_coverage(results, intent)
          )

  ---
  6. PLANNING & REASONING SYSTEM

  6.1 ReAct Loop Implementation

  # services/planner/src/react_loop.py
  class ReActAgent:
      """
      Implements ReAct (Reason + Act) paradigm.
      """

      SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are an autonomous agent with the following cycle:
      
      1. THINK: Analyze the current situation and reason about next action
      2. ACT: Execute a tool with specific parameters
      3. OBSERVE: Analyze the result of your action
      4. REFLECT: Decide if goal is achieved or more actions needed
      
      You have access to these tools:
      - search_web(query): Search the internet
      - search_knowledge(query): Search your knowledge base
      - retrieve_memories(query): Retrieve relevant memories
      - execute_code(code): Run Python code
      - schedule_task(task, time): Schedule a task
      - send_notification(message, channel): Send notification
      - create_plan(subgoals): Create a sub-plan
      
      Always output your reasoning in the 'thought' field.
      """

      async def run(self, goal: str, max_iterations: int = 20) ->
  ExecutionResult:
          observations = []
          history = []

          for i in range(max_iterations):
              # Build context from history
              context = self._build_context(goal, observations, history)

              # Get next action from LLM
              action = await self._decide_action(context)

              if action.type == "FINISH":
                  return ExecutionResult(
                      success=True,
                      steps=history,
                      final_output=action.output
                  )

              # Execute action
              result = await self._execute_action(action)
              observations.append({
                  "action": action.type,
                  "params": action.params,
                  "result": result
              })
              history.append(action)

              # Check for loops
              if self._detect_loop(history):
                  # Trigger alternative planning
                  alt_plan = await self._replan(goal, history)
                  if alt_plan:
                      history.extend(alt_plan)

          return ExecutionResult(
              success=False,
              steps=history,
              error="Max iterations reached"
          )

  6.2 Tree-of-Thought Implementation

  # services/planner/src/tree_of_thought.py
  class TreeOfThoughtPlanner:
      """
      Parallel exploration of multiple reasoning paths.
      """

      async def plan(
          self,
          goal: str,
          num_branches: int = 3,
          depth_limit: int = 5
      ) -> PlanResult:

          # Root node
          root = ThoughtNode(
              goal=goal,
              reasoning="Starting planning",
              depth=0,
              path=[]
          )

          # BFS expansion
          queue = [root]
          all_leaves = []

          while queue and len(all_leaves) < num_branches * 2:
              node = queue.pop(0)

              if node.depth >= depth_limit:
                  all_leaves.append(node)
                  continue

              # Generate candidate branches
              branches = await self._generate_branches(node)

              for branch in branches:
                  child = ThoughtNode(
                      goal=goal,
                      reasoning=branch.reasoning,
                      depth=node.depth + 1,
                      path=node.path + [branch],
                      parent=node,
                      evaluation=branch.score
                  )
                  node.children.append(child)

                  if branch.is_terminal:
                      all_leaves.append(child)
                  else:
                      queue.append(child)

          # Score and select best path
          scored_paths = []
          for leaf in all_leaves:
              score = await self._evaluate_path(leaf)
              path = self._reconstruct_path(leaf)
              scored_paths.append((score, path))

          scored_paths.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
          best_score, best_path = scored_paths[0]

          return PlanResult(
              plan=best_path,
              alternative_paths=scored_paths[1:3],
              evaluation=best_score
          )

  ---
  7. REAL ORCHESTRATION LAYER

  7.1 Technology Stack Selection

  Decision Matrix

  Requirement: Durable Workflow Execution
  Technology: Temporal
  Decision: Temporal
  Rationale: Best-in-class durable execution with built-in retries, sagas,
    activity tracking
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Requirement: Agent Orchestration
  Technology: LangGraph
  Decision: Temporal SDK + Custom
  Rationale: LangGraph lacks durability; use Temporal for workflow, custom for
    agent cognition
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Requirement: Message Queue
  Technology: NATS
  Decision: NATS JetStream
  Rationale: <1ms latency, native pub/sub, exactly-once, multi-tenant
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Requirement: Distributed Processing
  Technology: Ray
  Decision: Ray (optional)
  Rationale: Only if GPU workloads needed; otherwise overkill
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Requirement: Workflow Definition
  Technology: Temporal
  Decision: Temporal
  Rationale: Native workflow definitions with Go/Python SDK
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Requirement: Job Queue
  Technology: Temporal
  Decision: Temporal
  Rationale: Temporal activities replace Celery/Prefect

  Why NOT Kafka: Operational complexity too high for this scale. NATS is
  sufficient.

  Why NOT Prefect/Airflow: No durable execution. Task fails = lost work.

  Why NOT LangGraph alone: No persistence, no retries, no distributed execution.

  7.2 Temporal Workflow Definition

  # services/workflows/src/workflows/interview_prep.py
  from temporalio import workflow
  from datetime import timedelta
  import asyncio

  @workflow.defn
  class InterviewPrepWorkflow:
      """
      Durable workflow for ML interview preparation.
      Survives server restarts, retries failed activities.
      """

      @workflow.run
      async def run(self, user_id: str, job_description: str) -> PrepResult:
          # Track state across restarts
          state = await workflow.execute_activity(
              InitializeState,
              user_id,
              start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(seconds=30)
          )

          # Step 1: Assess current level
          assessment = await workflow.execute_activity(
              AssessMLLevel,
              AssessInput(user_id=user_id, job_desc=job_description),
              start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(minutes=5),
              retry_policy=RetryPolicy(maximum_attempts=2)
          )

          # Step 2: Create personalized study plan
          plan = await workflow.execute_activity(
              CreateStudyPlan,
              PlanInput(
                  user_id=user_id,
                  assessment=assessment,
                  job_description=job_description
              ),
              start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(minutes=3)
          )

          # Step 3: Schedule daily coaching sessions (parallel activities)
          schedule_tasks = [
              workflow.execute_activity(
                  ScheduleCoachingSession,
                  ScheduleInput(user_id=user_id, date=date, topics=topics),
                  start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(minutes=2),
                  schedule_to_close_timeout=timedelta(hours=1)  # Allow for 
  scheduling delay
              )
              for date, topics in plan.daily_sessions
          ]
          await asyncio.gather(*schedule_tasks)

          # Step 4: Set up progress tracking
          await workflow.execute_activity(
              SetupProgressTracking,
              ProgressInput(user_id=user_id, plan_id=plan.plan_id),
              start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(minutes=2)
          )

          # Step 5: Send initial notification
          await workflow.execute_activity(
              SendWelcomeNotification,
              user_id,
              start_to_close_timeout=timedelta(seconds=30)
          )

          # Step 6: Start background monitoring (continues after workflow)
          workflow.execute_child_workflow(
              MonitorProgressWorkflow,
              MonitorInput(user_id=user_id, plan_id=plan.plan_id),
              id=f"monitor-{user_id}-{plan.plan_id}",
              parent_close_policy=ParentClosePolicy.REQUEST_CANCEL
          )

          return PrepResult(
              plan_id=plan.plan_id,
              sessions_scheduled=len(plan.daily_sessions),
              estimated_duration=plan.total_duration,
              next_session=plan.daily_sessions[0]
          )

  8. MEMORY & DATA LAYER

  8.1 PostgreSQL Schema

  -- services/database/schema.sql

  -- Enable required extensions
  CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS vector;
  CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
  CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm;

  -- Tenants
  CREATE TABLE tenants (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      plan VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'free',
      settings JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  -- Users
  CREATE TABLE users (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id),
      email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      display_name VARCHAR(255),
      role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'user',
      metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      UNIQUE(tenant_id, email)
  );

  -- Sessions
  CREATE TABLE sessions (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      token_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      refresh_token_hash VARCHAR(255),
      expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      last_active_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
  );

  -- Episodic Memory
  CREATE TABLE episodic_memories (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      content JSONB NOT NULL,
      importance FLOAT DEFAULT 0.5,
      emotional_tone VARCHAR(50),
      topics TEXT[],
      episode_type VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'conversation',
      outcome VARCHAR(50),
      source VARCHAR(100),
      started_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      ended_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      archived_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      summary TEXT,
      embedding VECTOR(1536)
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_episodic_user_time ON episodic_memories(user_id, created_at
  DESC);
  CREATE INDEX idx_episodic_topics ON episodic_memories USING GIN(topics);
  CREATE INDEX idx_episodic_embedding ON episodic_memories USING
  ivfflat(embedding vector_cosine_ops);

  -- Semantic Memory (Facts & Knowledge)
  CREATE TABLE semantic_memories (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      content TEXT NOT NULL,
      embedding VECTOR(1536),
      confidence FLOAT DEFAULT 1.0,
      importance FLOAT DEFAULT 0.5,
      fact_type VARCHAR(50),
      source_episodes UUID[],
      category VARCHAR(100),
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      last_accessed TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      access_count INT DEFAULT 0,
      decay_score FLOAT DEFAULT 1.0
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_semantic_user ON semantic_memories(user_id);
  CREATE INDEX idx_semantic_embedding ON semantic_memories USING
  ivfflat(embedding vector_cosine_ops);
  CREATE INDEX idx_semantic_category ON semantic_memories(user_id, category);
  CREATE INDEX idx_semantic_trgm ON semantic_memories USING GIN(content
  gin_trgm_ops);

  -- Knowledge Graph (Relationships)
  CREATE TABLE knowledge_nodes (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      node_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
      name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      properties JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      embedding VECTOR(1536),
      importance FLOAT DEFAULT 0.5,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  CREATE TABLE knowledge_edges (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      source_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES knowledge_nodes(id),
      target_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES knowledge_nodes(id),
      relationship VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
      weight FLOAT DEFAULT 1.0,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      UNIQUE(source_id, target_id, relationship)
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_edges_source ON knowledge_edges(source_id);
  CREATE INDEX idx_edges_target ON knowledge_edges(target_id);

  -- Procedural Memory
  CREATE TABLE procedures (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      trigger_conditions JSONB NOT NULL,
      steps JSONB NOT NULL,
      success_rate FLOAT DEFAULT 0.0,
      usage_count INT DEFAULT 0,
      last_used_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  -- Working Memory (Redis-backed, PostgreSQL checkpoint)
  CREATE TABLE working_memory_checkpoints (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      session_id UUID NOT NULL,
      content JSONB NOT NULL,
      checkpoint_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_working_session ON working_memory_checkpoints(user_id,
  session_id);

  -- Documents
  CREATE TABLE documents (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
      source VARCHAR(100),
      source_url TEXT,
      content TEXT,
      embedding VECTOR(1536),
      metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_documents_user ON documents(user_id);
  CREATE INDEX idx_documents_embedding ON documents USING ivfflat(embedding
  vector_cosine_ops);

  -- Document Chunks
  CREATE TABLE document_chunks (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      document_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES documents(id),
      chunk_index INT NOT NULL,
      content TEXT NOT NULL,
      embedding VECTOR(1536),
      metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_chunks_doc ON document_chunks(document_id);
  CREATE INDEX idx_chunks_embedding ON document_chunks USING ivfflat(embedding
  vector_cosine_ops);

  -- Agent Executions
  CREATE TABLE agent_executions (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      workflow_id UUID,
      agent_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
      agent_id VARCHAR(255),
      state VARCHAR(50),
      input_payload JSONB,
      output_payload JSONB,
      error TEXT,
      started_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      duration_ms INT,
      token_usage JSONB,
      cost_usd FLOAT
  );

  CREATE INDEX idx_executions_user_time ON agent_executions(user_id, started_at
  DESC);
  CREATE INDEX idx_executions_workflow ON agent_executions(workflow_id);

  -- Vector Collections (for Qdrant metadata)
  CREATE TABLE vector_collections (
      id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
      user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
      collection_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
      dimension INT NOT NULL,
      description TEXT,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      config JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
  );

  8.2 Redis Strategy

  # services/redis/src/schemas.py
  # Working memory and session caching

  WORKING_MEMORY_SCHEMA = {
      "prefix": "wm:{tenant_id}:{user_id}",
      "ttl": 3600,  # 1 hour
      "structure": {
          "conversation": {
              "type": "list",
              "max_items": 1000,
              "item_schema": {
                  "role": "string",
                  "content": "string",
                  "timestamp": "int",
                  "tokens": "int"
              }
          },
          "context": {
              "type": "hash",
              "fields": {
                  "current_goal": "string",
                  "active_plan": "json",
                  "token_budget": "int",
                  "last_update": "int"
              }
          },
          "state": {
              "type": "hash",
              "fields": {
                  "agent_state": "string",
                  "cycle_number": "int",
                  "confidence": "float"
              }
          }
      }
  }

  SESSION_SCHEMA = {
      "prefix": "session:{session_id}",
      "ttl": 86400,  # 24 hours
      "structure": {
          "user_id": "string",
          "tenant_id": "string",
          "created_at": "int",
          "last_active": "int",
          "metadata": "json"
      }
  }

  # Lua script for atomic token budget deduction
  TOKEN_BUDGET_SCRIPT = """
  local key = KEYS[1]
  local cost = tonumber(ARGV[1])
  local budget = tonumber(redis.call('HGET', key, 'token_budget') or '0')
  if budget >= cost then
      redis.call('HSET', key, 'token_budget', budget - cost)
      return budget - cost
  else
      return -1  -- Insufficient budget
  end
  """

  9. SECURITY ARCHITECTURE

  9.1 Security Layers

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ                         SECURITY LAYERS                                  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Ө
  в”Ӯ                                                                          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  LAYER 1: NETWORK SECURITY                                               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  - TLS 1.3 everywhere                                           в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  - VPC/private subnets for services                             в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  - Security groups / firewall rules                            в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ  - DDoS protection (CloudFlare/Akamai)                         в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ

  9.2 Prompt Injection Defense

  # services/security/src/prompt_injection_detector.py
  class PromptInjectionDetector:
      """
      Multi-layer defense against prompt injection attacks.
      """

      def __init__(self):
          self.injection_patterns = [

  r"(?i)(ignore\s+(previous|all|my)\s+(instructions?|rules?|constraints?))",

  r"(?i)(forget\s+(everything|all|what)\s+(you|I've)\s+(told|said))",
              r"(?i)(you\s+are\s+now\s+(a\s+)?(different|new|another))",
              r"(?i)(system\s*prompt\s*(leak|extraction|injection))",
              r"(?i)(pretend\s+you\s+(are|can)\s+ignore)",
              r"(?i)(DAN\s+do\s+anything\s+now)",
              r"<\|system\|>|<\|user\|>|<\|assistant\|>",
              r"\[INST\]|\[/INST\]|\<\<SYS\>\>",
          ]

          self.boundary_markers = ["<|reserved_20097|>"]

      async def detect(self, text: str) -> InjectionResult:
          matches = []
          confidence = 0.0

          # Pattern matching
          for i, pattern in enumerate(self.injection_patterns):
              found = re.finditer(pattern, text)
              for match in found:
                  matches.append({
                      "pattern_id": i,
                      "match": match.group(),
                      "position": match.start(),
                      "severity": self._severity_for_pattern(i)
                  })
                  confidence += 0.3

          # Boundary marker detection
          for marker in self.boundary_markers:
              if marker in text:
                  matches.append({
                      "type": "boundary_marker",
                      "marker": marker,
                      "severity": "high"
                  })
                  confidence += 0.4

          # Token analysis (model-based)
          token_analysis = await self._analyze_tokens(text)
          if token_analysis.get("suspicious_tokens", 0) > 3:
              confidence += 0.2

          return InjectionResult(
              is_injection=confidence > 0.5,
              confidence=min(confidence, 1.0),
              matches=matches,
              sanitized_text=self._sanitize(text, matches)
          )

      def _sanitize(self, text: str, matches: list) -> str:
          """Remove or escape detected injection patterns"""
          sanitized = text
          for match in matches:
              if match.get("severity") == "critical":
                  sanitized = sanitized.replace(match["match"], "[FILTERED]")
          return sanitized

  ---
  10. RELIABILITY & FAULT TOLERANCE

  10.1 Circuit Breaker Implementation

  # services/resilience/src/circuit_breaker.py
  from enum import Enum
  from datetime import datetime, timedelta
  from dataclasses import dataclass
  import asyncio

  class CircuitState(Enum):
      CLOSED = "closed"      # Normal operation
      OPEN = "open"          # Failing, reject requests
      HALF_OPEN = "half_open"  # Testing recovery

  @dataclass
  class CircuitBreakerConfig:
      failure_threshold: int = 5      # Open after 5 failures
      success_threshold: int = 2       # Close after 2 successes (half-open)
      timeout_seconds: float = 30.0   # Stay open for 30 seconds
      half_open_max_calls: int = 3    # Max concurrent calls in half-open

  class CircuitBreaker:
      def __init__(self, name: str, config: CircuitBreakerConfig):
          self.name = name
          self.config = config
          self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
          self.failure_count = 0
          self.success_count = 0
          self.last_failure_time: datetime = None
          self.half_open_calls = 0

      async def call(self, func, *args, **kwargs):
          if self.state == CircuitState.OPEN:
              if self._should_attempt_reset():
                  self.state = CircuitState.HALF_OPEN
                  self.half_open_calls = 0
              else:
                  raise CircuitOpenError(f"Circuit {self.name} is OPEN")

          if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
              if self.half_open_calls >= self.config.half_open_max_calls:
                  raise CircuitOpenError(f"Circuit {self.name} half-open limit
  reached")
              self.half_open_calls += 1

          try:
              result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
              self._on_success()
              return result
          except Exception as e:
              self._on_failure()
              raise

      def _on_success(self):
          self.failure_count = 0
          if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
              self.success_count += 1
              if self.success_count >= self.config.success_threshold:
                  self.state = CircuitState.CLOSED
                  self.success_count = 0
          elif self.state == CircuitState.CLOSED:
              self.success_count = 0

      def _on_failure(self):
          self.failure_count += 1
          self.last_failure_time = datetime.utcnow()

          if self.state == CircuitState.HALF_OPEN:
              self.state = CircuitState.OPEN
              self.success_count = 0
          elif self.failure_count >= self.config.failure_threshold:
              self.state = CircuitState.OPEN

      def _should_attempt_reset(self) -> bool:
          if not self.last_failure_time:
              return True
          elapsed = (datetime.utcnow() - self.last_failure_time).total_seconds()
          return elapsed >= self.config.timeout_seconds

  10.2 Provider Fallback Strategy

  # services/llm-gateway/src/provider_manager.py
  class LLMProviderManager:
      """
      Multi-provider routing with automatic failover.
      """

      def __init__(self):
          self.providers: dict[str, LLMProvider] = {}
          self.circuit_breakers: dict[str, CircuitBreaker] = {}
          self.health_status: dict[str, HealthStatus] = {}
          self.fallback_chain = [
              "anthropic",
              "openai",
              "nvidia",
              "google",
              "deepseek"
          ]

      async def complete(
          self,
          messages: list[dict],
          model_preference: str = None,
          **kwargs
      ) -> LLMResponse:

          providers_to_try = self._get_provider_chain(model_preference)
          last_error = None

          for provider_name in providers_to_try:
              breaker = self.circuit_breakers.get(provider_name)
              provider = self.providers.get(provider_name)

              if not provider or breaker.state == CircuitState.OPEN:
                  continue

              try:
                  result = await breaker.call(
                      provider.complete,
                      messages,
                      **kwargs
                  )
                  await self._record_success(provider_name)
                  return result

              except CircuitOpenError:
                  continue
              except ProviderError as e:
                  await self._record_failure(provider_name, e)
                  last_error = e
                  continue

          raise AllProvidersFailedError(
              f"All LLM providers failed. Last error: {last_error}"
          )

      async def _record_success(self, provider: str):
          self.health_status[provider] = HealthStatus(
              available=True,
              latency_p50=self._update_latency(provider),
              error_rate=self._update_error_rate(provider, False)
          )

      async def _record_failure(self, provider: str, error: Exception):
          self.health_status[provider] = HealthStatus(
              available=self.circuit_breakers[provider].state !=
  CircuitState.OPEN,
              latency_p50=self.health_status.get(provider,
  HealthStatus()).latency_p50,
              error_rate=self._update_error_rate(provider, True),
              last_error=str(error)
          )

  ---

  в”ҳ

  11.2 Token Budget Management

  # services/llm-gateway/src/token_budget.py
  class TokenBudgetManager:
      """
      Manages token budgets per user to prevent runaway costs.
      """

      def __init__(self, redis: Redis, db: Database):
          self.redis = redis
          self.db = db
          self.default_budget = 10_000_000  # 10M tokens/month

      async def check_and_reserve(
          self,
          user_id: str,
          estimated_tokens: int
      ) -> tuple[bool, BudgetInfo]:
          """
          Atomically check budget and reserve tokens.
          Returns (allowed, budget_info)
          """
          key = f"budget:{user_id}"

          # Get current usage
          usage = await self.redis.hgetall(key)
          used = int(usage.get(b"used", 0))
          budget = int(usage.get(b"budget", self.default_budget))
          reset_at = int(usage.get(b"reset_at", 0))

          # Check reset
          if time.time() > reset_at:
              used = 0
              reset_at = self._next_reset_timestamp()
              await self.redis.hset(key, mapping={
                  "used": 0,
                  "budget": budget,
                  "reset_at": reset_at
              })

          remaining = budget - used

          if estimated_tokens > remaining:
              return False, BudgetInfo(
                  budget=budget,
                  used=used,
                  remaining=remaining,
                  reset_at=reset_at,
                  over_limit_by=estimated_tokens - remaining
              )

          # Reserve tokens
          new_used = await self.redis.hincrby(key, "used", estimated_tokens)

          # Persist to database
          await self.db.execute(
              """
              INSERT INTO token_usage (user_id, tokens_used, recorded_at)
              VALUES ($1, $2, NOW())
              ON CONFLICT (user_id, date_trunc('day', recorded_at))
              DO UPDATE SET tokens_used = token_usage.tokens_used + $2
              """,
              user_id, estimated_tokens
          )

          return True, BudgetInfo(
              budget=budget,
              used=new_used,
              remaining=budget - new_used,
              reset_at=reset_at,
              over_limit_by=0
          )

  в”ҳ

  12.2 AI-Specific Telemetry

  # services/observability/src/ai_telemetry.py
  from opentelemetry import trace
  from opentelemetry.trace import SpanKind

  class AITelemetry:
      """
      AI-specific observability for Langfuse-style tracing.
      """

      def __init__(self, langfuse_client):
          self.langfuse = langfuse_client
          self.tracer = trace.get_tracer(__name__)

      async def trace_agent_execution(
          self,
          agent_id: str,
          goal: str,
          model: str,
          user_id: str
      ) -> ContextManager:
          """
          Trace a complete agent execution with all LLM calls,
          tool usages, and state transitions.
          """
          return self.tracer.start_as_current_span(
              f"agent.{agent_id}",
              kind=SpanKind.INTERNAL,
              attributes={
                  "agent.id": agent_id,
                  "agent.goal": goal,
                  "llm.model": model,
                  "user.id": user_id,
                  "user.tier": await self._get_user_tier(user_id)
              }
          )

      async def trace_llm_call(
          self,
          span: Span,
          provider: str,
          model: str,
          messages: list[dict],
          response: dict,
          latency_ms: float
      ):
          """
          Record LLM call details for cost and quality tracking.
          """
          # Token usage
          input_tokens = response.get("usage", {}).get("prompt_tokens", 0)
          output_tokens = response.get("usage", {}).get("completion_tokens", 0)
          total_tokens = response.get("usage", {}).get("total_tokens", 0)

          span.set_attribute("llm.usage.input_tokens", input_tokens)
          span.set_attribute("llm.usage.output_tokens", output_tokens)
          span.set_attribute("llm.usage.total_tokens", total_tokens)
          span.set_attribute("llm.latency_ms", latency_ms)
          span.set_attribute("llm.provider", provider)
          span.set_attribute("llm.model", model)

          # Cost calculation
          cost = self._calculate_cost(provider, model, input_tokens,
  output_tokens)
          span.set_attribute("llm.cost_usd", cost)

          # Langfuse trace
          await self.langfuse.trace(
              name="llm_completion",
              user_id=span.attributes.get("user.id"),
              input=messages[-1]["content"] if messages else "",
              output=response.get("content", ""),
              metadata={
                  "provider": provider,
                  "model": model,
                  "latency_ms": latency_ms,
                  "tokens": total_tokens,
                  "cost_usd": cost
              }
          )

          # Update cumulative metrics
          await self._update_user_metrics(
              span.attributes["user.id"],
              tokens=total_tokens,
              cost=cost
          )

      async def detect_hallucination(
          self,
          response: str,
          context: list[str],
          user_id: str
      ) -> HallucinationResult:
          """
          Detect potential hallucinations using confidence scoring.
          """
          # Check against retrieved context
          if not context:
              confidence = 0.5  # Low confidence without context
          else:
              # Use LLM to check consistency
              consistency_score = await self._check_consistency(
                  response, context
              )
              confidence = consistency_score

          if confidence < 0.7:
              # Flag for human review or add disclaimer
              await self._flag_for_review(
                  user_id=user_id,
                  response=response,
                  confidence=confidence,
                  context=context
              )

          return HallucinationResult(
              confidence=confidence,
              is_flagged=confidence < 0.7,
              check_method="llm_consistency"
          )

  ---

  13.2 Real-Time Agent Visualization

  // frontend/components/AgentExecutionVisualizer.tsx
  "use client";

  import { useAgentStream } from "@/hooks/useAgentStream";

  export function AgentExecutionVisualizer({ sessionId }: { sessionId: string })
   {
    const { events, status } = useAgentStream(sessionId);

    return (
      <div className="agent-visualizer">
        {/* Agent State Timeline */}
        <div className="timeline">
          {events.map((event, i) => (
            <div key={i} className={`event event-${event.type}`}>
              <div className="event-marker" />
              <div className="event-content">
                <div className="event-header">
                  <span className="event-agent">{event.agent}</span>
                  <span 
  className="event-time">{formatTime(event.timestamp)}</span>
                </div>

                {event.type === "thinking" && (
                  <div className="thinking-block">
                    <div className="chain-of-thought">
                      {event.reasoning.map((step, j) => (
                        <div key={j} className="reasoning-step">
                          <span className="step-number">{j + 1}</span>
                          <span className="step-text">{step}</span>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}

                {event.type === "tool_call" && (
                  <div className="tool-call">
                    <span className="tool-name">{event.tool}</span>
                    <pre className="tool-input">{JSON.stringify(event.input,
  null, 2)}</pre>
                    <pre className="tool-output">{JSON.stringify(event.output,
  null, 2)}</pre>
                  </div>
                )}

                {event.type === "memory_access" && (
                  <div className="memory-access">
                    <span className="memory-type">{event.memoryType}</span>
                    <span className="memory-count">{event.retrieved}
  items</span>
                  </div>
                )}

                {event.type === "output" && (
                  <div className="agent-output">
                    <StreamingText text={event.content} />
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Token Budget Indicator */}
        <div className="token-budget">
          <div className="budget-bar">
            <div 
              className="budget-used" 
              style={{ width: `${(status.usedTokens / status.maxTokens) * 100}%`
   }}
            />
          </div>
          <div className="budget-labels">
            <span>Used: {status.usedTokens.toLocaleString()}</span>
            <span>Budget: {status.maxTokens.toLocaleString()}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  ---
  14. PRODUCTION INFRASTRUCTURE

  14.1 Kubernetes Deployment

  # infrastructure/kubernetes/base/values.yaml
  # Helm chart configuration for RasoSpeak AI Platform

  global:
    imageRegistry: ghcr.io
    imagePullSecrets: []
    storageClass: standard-ssd

  # API Gateway
  kong:
    enabled: true
    replicaCount: 3
    autoscaling:
      enabled: true
      minReplicas: 3
      maxReplicas: 20
      targetCPUUtilizationPercentage: 70
    resources:
      limits:
        cpu: 2000m
        memory: 2Gi
      requests:
        cpu: 500m
        memory: 512Mi

  # Agent Runtime Service
  agent-runtime:
    enabled: true
    replicaCount: 5
    autoscaling:
      enabled: true
      minReplicas: 5
      maxReplicas: 50
      # Scale based on active agent count
      metrics:
        - type: External
          external:
            metric:
              name: active_agents
            target:
              type: AverageValue
              averageValue: "50"
    resources:
      limits:
        cpu: 4000m
        memory: 8Gi
      requests:
        cpu: 1000m
        memory: 2Gi

  # GPU Nodes for vLLM inference
  gpu-node-pool:
    enabled: true
    nodePoolName: gpu-pool
    machineType: a2-highgpu-1g  # 1x NVIDIA A100
    autoscaling:
      minNodes: 1
      maxNodes: 10
    taints:
      - key: "nvidia.com/gpu"
        value: "present"
        effect: "NoSchedule"

  # Memory Service
  memory-service:
    enabled: true
    replicaCount: 3
    database:
      # PostgreSQL with pgvector
      postgresql:
        enabled: true
        auth:
          database: rasospeak
          username: rasospeak
        primary:
          persistence:
            enabled: true
            size: 100Gi
          resources:
            limits:
              cpu: 4000m
              memory: 16Gi
        readReplicas:
          replicaCount: 2
          persistence:
            enabled: true
            size: 100Gi

  # Redis
  redis:
    enabled: true
    architecture: replication
    auth:
      enabled: true
    master:
      persistence:
        enabled: true
        size: 10Gi
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 4Gi
    replica:
      replicaCount: 2
      persistence:
        enabled: true
        size: 10Gi

  # Qdrant Vector DB
  qdrant:
    enabled: true
    persistence:
      enabled: true
      size: 50Gi
    resources:
      limits:
        memory: 8Gi

  # Temporal
  temporal:
    enabled: true
    server:
      frontend:
        replicaCount: 3
      history:
        replicaCount: 3
      matching:
        replicaCount: 3
      worker:
        replicaCount: 5
    cassandra:
      enabled: true
      persistence:
        enabled: true
        size: 200Gi

  # NATS JetStream
  nats:
    enabled: true
    replicaCount: 3
    jetstream:
      enabled: true
      persistence:
        enabled: true
        size: 50Gi

  # Service Mesh (Istio)
  istio:
    enabled: true
    global:
      mtls:
        mode: STRICT
    ingress:
      enabled: true
      gateways:
        - name: rasospeak-gateway
          tls:
            mode: SIMPLE
            credentialName: rasospeak-tls
      hosts:
        - "api.rasospeak.ai"
        - "app.rasospeak.ai"

  # Monitoring
  prometheus:
    enabled: true
    alertmanager:
      enabled: true
    server:
      retention: 30d

  grafana:
    enabled: true
    persistence:
      enabled: true
      size: 10Gi

  15. AI INFRASTRUCTURE STACK

  15.1 Complete Technology Stack Decision

  Category: Agent Orchestration
  Technology: Temporal SDK + Custom
  Decision: Temporal
  Rationale: Durable execution critical; LangGraph lacks persistence
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Memory Systems
  Technology: PostgreSQL + pgvector + Redis
  Decision: Tiered
  Rationale: Working=Redis, Episodic=pgvector, Semantic=pgvector
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Workflow Execution
  Technology: Temporal
  Decision: Temporal
  Rationale: Non-negotiable for durable execution
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: AI Observability
  Technology: Langfuse + OpenTelemetry
  Decision: Langfuse
  Rationale: Best AI-specific tracing and evaluation
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Vector Search
  Technology: Qdrant
  Decision: Qdrant
  Rationale: Performance + hybrid search + operational simplicity
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Speech Systems
  Technology: Whisper + Cartesia
  Decision: Hybrid
  Rationale: Self-hosted Whisper, cloud TTS
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Realtime Streaming
  Technology: Native WebSocket
  Decision: Native
  Rationale: Avoid Socket.io overhead for streaming
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Multi-Provider LLM
  Technology: LiteLLM
  Decision: LiteLLM
  Rationale: Unified interface across 100+ providers
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Category: Long-term Memory
  Technology: PostgreSQL + S3
  Decision: PostgreSQL + S3
  Rationale: Structured data in Postgres, blobs in S3
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Technology: CrewAI

  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Technology: Haystack

  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  Technology: Prefect/Airflow
  Why Not: No durable execution; tasks fail = lost work
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Technology: Pinecone
  Why Not: Expensive at scale; Qdrant/Weaviate better value
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Technology: LangSmith

  16. REFACTOR & MIGRATION PLAN

  16.1 Phased Migration Strategy

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”җ
  в”Ӯ                    5-PHASE MIGRATION ROADMAP
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”Ө
  в”Ӯ                                                                            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  PHASE 1: STABILIZATION (Weeks 1-4)                                        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ                                                                            в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    - Each request gets fresh context                                      в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                                                            в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ    - Queue message retry                                                   в”Ӯ
